passes with leader election to ensure\n380\t/// only one pod runs the fingerprinting at a time.\n381\tpub struct AntiEntropyWorker {\n382\t    config: AntiEntropyWorkerConfig,\n383\t    reconciler: AntiEntropyReconciler<HttpNodeClient>,\n384\t    topology: Arc<RwLock<Topology>>,\n385\t    task_store: Arc<dyn TaskStore>,\n386\t    pod_id: String,\n387\t    /// Total shards in the cluster (for scaling.\n392\t    num_pods: Option<u32>,\n393\t    /// RF (replication factor) for Mode A scaling.\n394\t    rf: usize,\n395\t    /// Whether TTL is enabled for expired document handling (plan §13.14 interaction).\n396\t    ttl_enabled: bool,\n397\t    /// Metrics callback for shards scanned.\n398\t    metrics_shards_scanned: Option<Arc<dyn Fn(u64) + Send + Sync>>,\n399\t    /// Metrics callback {\n408\t    /// Create a new anti-entropy worker.\n409\t    pub fn new(\n410\t        config: AntiEntropyWorkerConfig,\n411\t        topology: Arc<RwLock<Topology>>,\n412\t        task_store: Arc<dyn TaskStore>,\n413\t        node_master_key: String,\n414\t        pod_id: String,\n415\t    ) -> Self {\n416\t        let ae_config = AntiEntropyConfig {\n417\t            enabled: true,\n418\t            schedule: format!(\"every {}s\", config.interval_s),\n419\t            index_uid: \"default\".to_string(),\n420\t            shards_per_pass: 0, // Scan all shards\n421\t            max_read_concurrency: 2,\n422\t            fingerprint_batch_size: 1000,\n423\t            auto_repair: true,\n424\t            updated_at_field: \"_miroir_updated_at\".to_string(),\n425\t            expires_at_field: \"_miroir_expires_at\".to_string(),\n426\t            ttl_enabled: false, // Will be updated by set_ttl_enabled\n427\t        };\n428\t\n429\t        let node_client = Arc::new(node_client),\n434\t        );\n435\t\n436\t        Self {\n437\t            config,\n438\t            reconciler,\n439\t            topology,\n440\t            task_store,\n441\t RF\n446\t            ttl_enabled: false,\n447\t            metrics_shards_scanned: None,\n448\t            metrics_mismatches_found: None,\n449\t            metrics_docs_repaired: None,\n450\t            metrics_scan_completed: None,\n451\t        }\n452\t    }\n453\t\n454\t    /// Set Mode A scaling parameters (plan §14.6).\n455\t    ///\n456\t    /// When enabled, each pod fingerprints and repairs only its rendezvous-owned shards.\n457\t    ///\n458\t    /// # Parameters\n459\t    ///\n460\t    /// - `replica_group_id`: This pod's ID in the pod pool (0-indexed)\n461\t    /// - `num_pods`: Total number of pods running anti-entropy\n462\t    pub fn with_mode_a_scaling(mut self, replica_group_id: u32, num_pods: u32) -> Self {\n463\t        self.replica_group_id = Some(replica_group_id);\n464\t        self.num_pods = Some(num_pods);\n465\t        self\n466\t    }\n467\t\n468\t    /// Set metrics callbacks.\n469\t    pub fn with_metrics(\n470\t        mut self,\n471\t        shards_scanned: Arc<dyn Fn(u64) + Send + Sync>,\n472\t        mismatches_found: Arc<dyn Fn(u64) + Send + Sync>,\n473\t        docs_repaired: Arc<dyn Fn(u64) + Send + Sync>,\n474\t        scan_completed: Arc<dyn Fn(u64) + Send + Sync>,\n475\t    ) -> Self {\n476\t        self.metrics_shards_scanned = Some(shards_scanned);\n477\t        self.metrics_mismatches_found = Some(mismatches_found);\n478\t        self.metrics_docs_repaired = Some(docs_repaired);\n479\t        self.metrics_scan_completed = Some(scan_completed);\n480\t        self\n481\t    }\n482\t\n483\t    /// Set whether TTL is enabled for expired document handling (plan §13.14 interaction).\n484\t    pub fn set_ttl_enabled(&mut self, enabled: bool) {\n485\t        self.ttl_enabled = enabled;\n486\t        // Update reconciler config to match\n487\t        self.reconciler.set_ttl_enabled(enabled);\n488\t    }\n489\t\n490\t    /// Start the background worker.\n491\t    ///\n492\t    /// This runs in a loop:\n493\t    /// 1. Try to acquire leader lease (scope: anti_entropy)\n494\t    /// 2. If acquired, run anti-entropy pass\n495\t    /// 3. Renew lease periodically\n496\t    /// 4. If lease lost, go back to step 1\n497\t    pub async fn run(&self) {\n498\t        info!(\n499\t            pod_id = %self.pod_id,\n500\t            interval_s = self.config.interval_s,\n501\t            \"anti-entropy worker starting\"\n502\t        );\n503\t\n504\t        let scope = \"anti_entropy\";\n505\t\n506\t        loop {\n507\t            let now_ms = now_ms();\n508\t            let expires_at = now_ms + (self.config.lease_ttl_secs * 1000) as i64;\n509\t\n510\t            // Try to acquire leader lease\n511\t            match tokio::task::spawn_blocking({\n512\t                let task_store = self.task_store.clone();\n513\t                let scope = scope.to_string();\n514\t                let pod_id = self.pod_id.clone();\n515\t                move || {\n516\t                    task_store.try_acquire_leader_lease(&scope, &pod_id, expires_at, now_ms)\n517\t                }\n518\t            })\n519\t            .await\n520\t            {\n521\t                Ok(Ok(true)) => {\n522\t                    info!(scope = %scope, pod_id = %self.pod_id, \"acquired leader lease\");\n523\t\n524\t                    // We are the leader - run anti-entropy pass cycle\n525\t                    if let Err(e) = self.run_pass_cycle().await {\n526\t                        error!(error = %e, \"anti-entropy pass cycle failed\");\n527\t                    }\n528\t                }\n529\t                Ok(Ok(false)) => {\n530\t                    debug!(scope = %scope, \"leader lease already held\");\n531\t                }\n532\t                Ok(Err(e)) => {\n533\t                    error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"failed to acquire leader lease\");\n534\t                }\n535\t                Err(e) => {\n536\t                    error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"spawn_blocking task failed\");\n537\t                }\n538\t            }\n539\t\n540\t            // Wait before retrying lease acquisition\n541\t            tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(\n542\t                self.config.lease_renewal_interval_ms,\n543\t            ))\n544\t            .await;\n545\t        }\n546\t    }\n547\t\n548\t    /// Run a single anti-entropy pass cycle.\n549\t    ///\n550\t    /// This runs the pass immediately after acquiring lease, then waits\n551\t    /// for the configured interval before running again (if still leader).\n552\t    async fn run_pass_cycle(&self) -> Result<(), String> {\n553\t        let scope = \"anti_entropy\";\n554\t        let mut lease_renewal = tokio::time::interval(Duration::from_millis(\n555\t            self.config.lease_renewal_interval_ms,\n556\t        ));\n557\t\n558\t        // Run anti-entropy pass immediately on acquiring lease\n559\t        self.run_single_pass().await?;\n560\t\n561\t        // Then wait for interval or lease expiry\n562\t        let pass_interval = tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_secs(self.config.interval_s));\n563\t\n564\t        tokio::select! {\n565\t            _ = lease_renewal.tick() => {\n566\t                // Renew lease\n567\t                let now_ms = now_ms();\n568\t                let expires_at = now_ms + (self.config.lease_ttl_secs * 1000) as i64;\n569\t\n570\t                match tokio::task::spawn_blocking({\n571\t                    let task_store = self.task_store.clone();\n572\t                    let scope = scope.to_string();\n573\t                    let pod_id = self.pod_id.clone();\n574\t                    move || {\n575\t                        task_store.renew_leader_lease(&scope, &pod_id, expires_at)\n576\t                    }\n577\t                })\n578\t                .await\n579\t                {\n580\t                    Ok(Ok(true)) => {\n581\t                        debug!(scope = %scope, \"renewed leader lease\");\n582\t                    }\n583\t                    Ok(Ok(false)) => {\n584\t                        info!(scope = %scope, \"lost leader lease\");\n585\t                        return Ok(());\n586\t                    }\n587\t                    Ok(Err(e)) => {\n588\t                        error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"failed to renew leader lease\");\n589\t                        return Err(e.to_string());\n590\t                    }\n591\t                    Err(e) => {\n592\t                        error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"spawn_blocking task failed\");\n593\t                        return Err(format!(\"spawn_blocking task failed: {}\", e));\n594\t                    }\n595\t                }\n596\t            }\n597\t            _ = pass_interval => {\n598\t                // Interval passed - run anti-entropy pass\n599\t                self.run_single_pass().await?;\n600\t            }\n601\t        }\n602\t\n603\t        Ok(())\n604\t    }\n605\t\n606\t    /// Run a single anti-entropy pass.\n607\t    async fn run_single_pass(&self) -> Result<(), String> {\n608\t        info!(\"starting anti-entropy pass\");\n609\t\n610\t        // Get topology info for Mode A scaling\n611\t        let (total_shards, rf) = {\n612\t            let topo = self.topology.read().await;\n613\t            (topo.shards, topo.rf())\n614\t        };\n615\t\n616\t        // Use the existing reconciler directly\n617\t        // Note: Mode A scaling and metrics are configured via worker fields,\n618\t        // not via the reconciler's builder pattern\n619\t        let reconciler = &self.reconciler;\n620\t\n621\t        match reconciler.run_pass().await {\n622\t            Ok(pass) => {\n623\t                info!(\n624\t                    shards_scanned = pass.shards_scanned,\n625\t                    shards_with_drift = pass.shards_with_drift,\n626\t                    repairs_performed = pass.repairs_performed,\n627\t                    errors = pass.errors.len(),\n628\t                    \"anti-entropy pass completed\"\n629\t                );\n630\t\n631\t                if !pass.errors.is_empty() {\n632\t                    warn!(errors = ?pass.errors, \"anti-entropy pass had errors\");\n633\t                }\n634\t\n635\t                // Emit worker-level metrics if callbacks are configured\n636\t                if let Some(ref callback) = self.metrics_shards_scanned {\n637\t                    callback(pass.shards_scanned as u64);\n638\t                }\n639\t                if let Some(ref callback) = self.metrics_scan_completed {\n640\t                    callback(pass.completed_at / 1000);\n641\t                }\n642\t\n643\t                Ok(())\n644\t            }\n645\t            Err(e) => {\n646\t                Err(format!(\"anti-entropy pass failed: {}\", e))\n647\t            }\n648\t        }\n649\t    }\n650\t}\n651\t\n652\t/// Get current time in milliseconds since Unix epoch.\n653\tfn now_ms() -> i64 {\n654\t    SystemTime::now()\n655\t        .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)\n656\t        .unwrap_or_default()\n657\t        .as_millis() as i64\n658\t}\n659\t\n660\t#[cfg(test)]\n661\tmod tests {\n662\t    use super::*;\n663\t\n664\t schedule.trim().to_lowercase();\n\n    // Match \"every X[unit]\" pattern\n    if !schedule.starts_with(\"every \") {\n        return None;\n    }\n\n    let rest = schedule[6..].trim();\n    if rest.is_empty() {\n        return None;\n    }\n\n    // Find the first non-digit character to split number from unit\n    let mut num_end = 0;\n    for (i, c) in rest.chars().enumerate() {\n        if !c.is_ascii_digit() {\n            num_end = i;\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if num_end == 0 {\n        return None;\n    }\n\n    let num_str = &rest[..num_end];\n    let unit = &rest[num_end..];\n\n    let value: u64 = num_str.parse().ok()?;\n\n    match unit {\n        \"s\" | \"sec\" | \"second\" | \"seconds\" => Some(value),\n        \"m\" | \"min\" | \"minute\" | \"minutes\" => Some(value * 60),\n        \"h\" | \"hour\" | \"hours\" => Some(value * 3600),\n        _ => None,\n    }\n}\n\n/// HTTP-based node client for anti-entropy fingerprinting.\n///\n/// Sync>>,\n}\n\nimpl AntiEntropyWorker {\n    /// Create a new anti-entropy worker.\n    pub fn new(\n        config: AntiEntropyWorkerConfig,\n        topology: Arc<RwLock<Topology>>,\n        task_store: Arc<dyn TaskStore>,\n        node_master_key: String,\n        pod_id: String,\n    ) -> Self {\n        let ae_config = AntiEntropyConfig {\n            enabled: true,\n            schedule: format!(\"every {}s\", config.interval_s),\n            index_uid: \"default\".to_string(),\n            shards_per_pass: 0, // Scan all shards\n            max_read_concurrency: 2,\n            fingerprint_batch_size: 1000,\n            auto_repair: true,\n            updated_at_field: \"_miroir_updated_at\".to_string(),\n            expires_at_field: \"_miroir_expires_at\".to_string(),\n            ttl_enabled: false, // Will be updated by set_ttl_enabled\n        };\n\n        let node_client = HttpNodeClient::new(node_master_key);\n        let reconciler,\n            topology,\n            task_store,\n            pod_id,\n            total_shards: 0, // Will be set when Mode A is enabled\n            replica_group_id: None,\n runs in a loop:\n    /// 1. Try to acquire leader lease (scope: anti_entropy)\n    /// 2. If acquired, run anti-entropy pass\n    /// 3. Renew lease periodically\n    /// 4. If lease lost, go back to step 1\n    pub async fn run(&self) {\n        info!(\n            pod_id = %self.pod_id,\n            interval_s = self.config.interval_s,\n            \"anti-entropy worker starting\"\n        );\n\n        let scope = \"anti_entropy\";\n\n        loop {\n            let now_ms = now_ms();\n            let expires_at = now_ms + (self.config.lease_ttl_secs * 1000) as i64;\n\n            // Try to acquire leader lease\n            match tokio::task::spawn_blocking({\n                let task_store = self.task_store.clone();\n                let scope = scope.to_string();\n                let pod_id = self.pod_id.clone();\n                move || {\n                    task_store.try_acquire_leader_lease(&scope, &pod_id, expires_at, now_ms)\n                }\n            })\n            .await\n            {\n                Ok(Ok(true)) => {\n                    info!(scope = %scope, pod_id = %self.pod_id, \"acquired leader lease\");\n\n                    // We are the leader - run anti-entropy pass cycle\n                    if let Err(e) = self.run_pass_cycle().await {\n                        error!(error = %e, \"anti-entropy pass cycle failed\");\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(Ok(false)) => {\n                    debug!(scope = %scope, \"leader lease already held\");\n                }\n                Ok(Err(e)) => {\n                    error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"failed to acquire leader lease\");\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"spawn_blocking task failed\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Wait before retrying lease acquisition\n            tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(\n                self.config.lease_renewal_interval_ms,\n            ))\n            .await;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Run a single anti-entropy pass cycle.\n    ///\n    /// This runs the pass immediately \"anti_entropy\";\n        let mut lease_renewal = tokio::time::interval(Duration::from_millis(\n            self.config.lease_renewal_interval_ms,\n        ));\n\n        // Run anti-entropy pass immediately on acquiring lease\n        self.run_single_pass().await?;\n\n        // Then wait for interval or lease expiry\n        let pass_interval = tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_secs(self.config.interval_s));\n\n        tokio::select! {\n            _ = lease_renewal.tick() => {\n                // Renew lease\n                let now_ms = now_ms();\n                let expires_at = now_ms + (self.config.lease_ttl_secs * 1000) as i64;\n\n                match tokio::task::spawn_blocking({\n                    let task_store = self.task_store.clone();\n                    let scope = scope.to_string();\n                    let pod_id = self.pod_id.clone();\n                    move || {\n                        task_store.renew_leader_lease(&scope, &pod_id, expires_at)\n                    }\n                })\n                .await\n                {\n                    Ok(Ok(true)) => {\n                        debug!(scope = %scope, \"renewed leader lease\");\n                    }\n                    Ok(Ok(false)) => {\n                        info!(scope = %scope, \"lost leader lease\");\n                        return Ok(());\n                    }\n                    Ok(Err(e)) => {\n                        error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"failed to renew leader lease\");\n                        return Err(e.to_string());\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        error!(scope = %scope, error = %e, \"spawn_blocking task failed\");\n                        return Err(format!(\"spawn_blocking task failed: {}\", e));\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            _ = pass_interval => {\n                // Interval passed - run anti-entropy pass\n                self.run_single_pass().await?;\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Run a single anti-entropy pass.\n    async fn run_single_pass(&self) -> Result<(), String> {\n        info!(\"starting anti-entropy pass\");\n\n        // Get topology info for Mode A scaling\n        let (total_shards, rf) = {\n            let topo = self.topology.read().await;\n            (topo.shards, topo.rf())\n        };\n\n        // Use the existing reconciler directly\n        // Note: Mode A scaling and metrics are configured via worker fields,\n        // not via the reconciler's builder pattern\n        let reconciler = &self.reconciler;\n\n        match reconciler.run_pass().await {\n            Ok(pass) => {\n                info!(\n                    shards_scanned = pass.shards_scanned,\n                    shards_with_drift = pass.shards_with_drift,\n                    repairs_performed = pass.repairs_performed,\n                    errors = pass.errors.len(),\n                    \"anti-entropy pass completed\"\n                );\n\n                if !pass.errors.is_empty() {\n                    warn!(errors = ?pass.errors, \"anti-entropy pass had errors\");\n                }\n\n                // Emit worker-level metrics if callbacks are configured\n                if let Some(ref callback) = self.metrics_shards_scanned {\n                    callback(pass.shards_scanned as u64);\n                }\n                if let Some(ref callback) = self.metrics_scan_completed {\n                    callback(pass.completed_at / 1000);\n                }\n\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                Err(format!(\"anti-entropy pass failed: {}\", e))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Get current time in milliseconds since Unix epoch.\nfn now_ms() -> i64 {\n    SystemTime::now()\n        .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)\n        .unwrap_or_default()\n        .as_millis() as i64\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_parse_schedule_interval_hours() {\n        assert_eq!(parse_schedule_interval(\"every 6h\"), self.topology.read().await;\n561\t        let shard_count = topology.shards;\n562\t        let replica_groups = topology.groups().count() as u32;\n563\t\n564\t        // Determine which shards to scan\n565\t        let all_shards: Vec<u32> = (0..shard_count).collect();\n566\t        let shards_to_scan = if let (Some(replica_group_id), Some(num_pods)) =\n567\t            (self.replica_group_id, self.num_pods)\n568\t        {\n569\t            // Mode A scaling: filter to rendezvous-owned shards\n570\t            all_shards\n571\t                .into_iter()\n572\t                .filter(|shard_id| {\n573\t                    // Shard belongs to this pod if shard_id % num_pods == replica_group_id\n574\t                    (*shard_id % num_pods) == replica_group_id\n575\t                })\n576\t                .collect()\n577\t        } else if self.config.shards_per_pass == 0 {\n578\t            // Scan all shards\n579\t            all_shards\n580\t        } else {\n581\t            // Scan a subset (for throttling)\n582\t            all_shards\n583\t                .into_iter()\n584\t                .take(self.config.shards_per_pass as usize)\n585\t                .collect()\n586\t        };\n587\t\n588\t        info!(\n589\t            \"Anti-entropy pass starting: {} shards to scan\",\n590\t            shards_to_scan.len()\n591\t        );\n592\t\n593\t        // Track total mismatches found\n594\t        let mut total_mismatches = 0u32;\n595\t\n596\t        // Scan each shard\n597\t        for shard_id in shards_to_scan {\n598\t            match self.scan_shard(&topology, shard_id).await {\n599\t                Ok((drift_detected, repairs, mismatches)) => {\n600\t                    pass.shards_scanned += 1;\n601\t                    if drift_detected {\n602\t                        pass.shards_with_drift += 1;\n603\t                    }\n604\t                    pass.repairs_performed += repairs;\n605\t                    total_mismatches += mismatches;\n606\t                }\n607\t                Err(e) => {\n608\t                    pass.errors.push(format!(\"shard {}: {}\", shard_id, e));\n609\t                }\n610\t            }\n611\t\n612\t            // Self-throttle: sleep between shards to target <2% CPU\n613\t            tokio::time::sleep(tokio::time::Duration::from_millis(100)).await;\n614\t        }\n615\t\n616\t        pass.completed_at = millis_now();\n617\t\n618\t        // Emit metrics if callback is configured\n619\t        if let Some(ref callback) = self.metrics_callback {\n620\t            callback(\n621\t                \"miroir_antientropy_shards_scanned_total\",\n622\t                pass.shards_scanned as u64,\n623\t            );\n624\t            callback(\n625\t                \"miroir_antientropy_mismatches_found_total\",\n626\t                total_mismatches as u64,\n627\t            );\n628\t            callback(\n629\t                \"miroir_antientropy_docs_repaired_total\",\n630\t                pass.repairs_performed as u64,\n631\t            );\n632\t            callback(\n633\t                \"miroir_antientropy_last_scan_completed_seconds\",\n634\t                pass.completed_at / 1000,\n635\t            );\n636\t        }\n637\t\n638\t        // Archive pass\n639\t        {\n640\t            let mut history = self.pass_history.write().await;\n641\t            history.push(pass.clone());\n642\t            // Keep last 100 passes\n643\t            if history.len() > 100 {\n644\t                history.remove(0);\n645\t            }\n646\t        }\n647\t\n648\t        // Clear current pass\n649\t        {\n650\t            let mut current = self.current_pass.write().await;\n651\t            *current = None;\n652\t        }\n653\t\n654\t        info!(\n655\t            \"Anti-entropy pass completed: {} shards scanned, {} with drift, {} repairs\",\n656\t            pass.shards_scanned, pass.shards_with_drift, pass.repairs_performed\n657\t        );\n658\t\n659\t        Ok(pass)\n660\t    }\n661\t\n662\t    /// Scan a single shard for drift.\n663\t    ///\n664\t    /// Returns (drift_detected, repairs_performed, mismatches_found).\n665\t    async fn scan_shard(&self, topology: &Topology, shard_id: u32) -> Result<(bool, u32, u32)> {\n666\t        // For each replica group, get the assigned nodes\n667\t        let mut fingerprints = Vec::new();\n668\t\n669\t        for group in topology.groups() {\n670\t            let assigned = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n671\t            for node_id in assigned {\n672\t                // Look up node address from topology\n673\t                let topology_guard = self.topology.read().await;\n674\t                let node = topology_guard\n675\t                    .node(&node_id)\n676\t                    .ok_or_else(|| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"node {} not found\", node_id)))?;\n677\t\n678\t                if !node.is_healthy() {\n679\t                    warn!(\"Node {} is not healthy, skipping fingerprint\", node_id);\n680\t                    continue;\n681\t                }\n682\t\n683\t                let address = node.address.clone();\n684\t                drop(topology_guard);\n685\t\n686\t                match self\n687\t                    .fingerprint_shard(&node_id, shard_id, &self.config.index_uid, &address)\n688\t                    .await\n689\t                {\n690\t                    Ok(fp) => fingerprints.push((node_id.clone(), address, fp)),\n691\t                    Err(e) => {\n692\t                        warn!(\n693\t                            \"Failed to fingerprint shard {} on node {}: {}\",\n694\t                            shard_id, node_id, e\n695\t                        );\n696\t                        // Continue with other nodes\n697\t                    }\n698\t                }\n699\t            }\n700\t        }\n701\t\n702\t        if fingerprints.is_empty() {\n703\t            // No readable replicas\n704\t            return Ok((false, 0, 0));\n705\t        }\n706\t\n707\t        // Compare fingerprints\n708\t        let (ref_node_id, ref_address, reference) = &fingerprints[0];\n709\t        let mut drift_detected = false;\n710\t        let mut repairs_performed = 0u32;\n711\t        let mut mismatches_found = 0u32;\n712\t\n713\t        for (node_id, address, fp) in &fingerprints[1..] {\n714\t            if fp.merkle_root != reference.merkle_root {\n715\t                drift_detected = true;\n716\t                debug!(\n717\t                    \"Shard {} drift detected: node {} has different merkle root\",\n718\t                    shard_id, node_id\n719\t                );\n720\t\n721\t                if self.config.auto_repair {\n722\t                    // Perform detailed diff and repair\n723\t                    match self\n724\t                        .repair_shard(\n725\t                            shard_id,\n726\t                            ref_node_id,\n727\t                            ref_address,\n728\t                            reference,\n729\t                            node_id,\n730\t                            address,\n731\t                            fp,\n732\t                        )\n733\t                        .await\n734\t                    {\n735\t                        Ok((repairs, mismatches)) => {\n736\t                            repairs_performed += repairs;\n737\t                            mismatches_found += mismatches;\n738\t                        }\n739\t                        Err(e) => {\n740\t                            error!(\n741\t                                \"Failed to repair shard {} on node {}: {}\",\n742\t                                shard_id, node_id, e\n743\t                            );\n744\t                        }\n745\t                    }\n746\t                }\n747\t            }\n748\t        }\n749\t\n750\t        Ok((drift_detected, repairs_performed, mismatches_found))\n751\t    }\n752\t\n753\t    /// Repair a shard by comparing replicas and applying fixes (plan §13.8 step 3).\n754\t    ///\n755\t    /// Returns (repairs_performed, mismatches_found).\n756\t    async fn repair_shard(\n757\t        &self,\n758\t        shard_id: u32,\n759\t        reference_node: &NodeId,\n760\t        reference_address: &str,\n761\t        reference_fp: &ShardFingerprint,\n762\t        target_node: &NodeId,\n763\t        target_address: &str,\n764\t        target_fp: &ShardFingerprint,\n765\t    ) -> Result<(u32, u32)> {\n766\t        debug!(\n767\t            \"Repairing shard {} on node {} (reference: node {})\",\n768\t            shard_id, target_node, reference_node\n769\t        );\n770\t\n771\t        // Step 1: Find divergent buckets using per-bucket hashes (plan §13.8 step 2)\n772\t        let divergent_buckets = self.diff_fingerprints(reference_fp, target_fp);\n773\t\n774\t        if divergent_buckets.is_empty() {\n775\t            // No bucket-level divergence (shouldn't happen if merkle roots differ)\n776\t            warn!(\n777\t                \"Shard {} merkle roots differ but no bucket divergence found\",\n778\t                shard_id\n779\t            );\n780\t            return Ok((0, 0));\n781\t        }\n782\t\n783\t        debug!(\n784\t            \"Shard {} has {} divergent buckets out of {}\",\n785\t            shard_id,\n786\t            divergent_buckets.len(),\n787\t            BUCKET_COUNT\n788\t        );\n789\t\n790\t        let mut total_repairs = 0u32;\n791\t        let mut total_mismatches = 0u32;\n792\t\n793\t        // Step 2: For each divergent bucket, enumerate divergent PKs\n794\t        for bucket_id in divergent_buckets {\n795\t            match self\n796\t                .compare_bucket_replicas(\n797\t                    shard_id,\n798\t                    bucket_id,\n799\t                    reference_node,\n800\t                    reference_address,\n801\t                    target_node,\n802\t                    target_address,\n803\t                    &self.config.index_uid,\n804\t                )\n805\t                .await\n806\t            {\n807\t                Ok(diff) => {\n808\t                    let total_divergent =\n809\t                        diff.a_only_pks.len() + diff.b_only_pks.len() + diff.mismatched_pks.len();\n810\t                    total_mismatches += total_divergent as u32;\n811\t\n812\t                    if total_divergent > 0 {\n813\t                        debug!(\n814\t                            \"Bucket {} in shard {}: {} divergent PKs ({} A-only, {} B-only, {} mismatched)\",\n815\t                            bucket_id,\n816\t                            shard_id,\n817\t                            total_divergent,\n818\t                            diff.a_only_pks.len(),\n819\t                            diff.b_only_pks.len(),\n820\t                            diff.mismatched_pks.len()\n821\t                        );\n822\t\n823\t                        // Step 3: For each divergent PK, apply repair (plan §13.8 step 3)\n824\t                        // Collect all divergent PKs\n825\t                        let mut all_divergent_pks = Vec::new();\n826\t                        all_divergent_pks.extend(diff.a_only_pks.iter().cloned());\n827\t                        all_divergent_pks.extend(diff.b_only_pks.iter().cloned());\n828\t                        all_divergent_pks.extend(diff.mismatched_pks.iter().cloned());\n829\t\n830\t                        // Repair each divergent PK\n831\t                        for pk in all_divergent_pks {\n832\t                            match self\n833\t                                .repair_divergent_pk(\n834\t                                    shard_id,\n835\t                                    &pk,\n836\t                                    reference_node,\n837\t                                    reference_address,\n838\t                                    target_node,\n839\t                                    target_address,\n840\t                                )\n841\t                                .await\n842\t                            {\n843\t                                Ok(repairs) => {\n844\t                                    total_repairs += repairs;\n845\t                                }\n846\t                                Err(e) => {\n847\t                                    error!(\n848\t                                        \"Failed to repair PK {} in shard {}: {}\",\n849\t                                        pk, shard_id, e\n850\t                                    );\n851\t                                }\n852\t                            }\n853\t                        }\n854\t                    }\n855\t                }\n856\t                Err(e) => {\n857\t                    warn!(\n858\t                        \"Failed to compare bucket {} in shard {}: {}\",\n859\t                        bucket_id, shard_id, e\n860\t                    );\n861\t                }\n862\t            }\n863\t        }\n864\t\n865\t        Ok((total_repairs, total_mismatches))\n866\t    }\n867\t\n868\t    /// Repair a single divergent primary key (plan §13.8 step 3).\n869\t    ///\n870\t    /// # Repair Logic (plan §13.8 step 3)\n871\t    ///\n872\t    /// For each divergent PK:\n873\t    /// 1. Read document from each replica\n874\t    /// 2. Check for TTL expiration:\n875\t    ///    - If ANY replica has `_miroir_expires_at <= now`: DELETE from all replicas\n876\t    ///    - This prevents zombie resurrection (plan §13.14 interaction)\n877\t    /// 3. Otherwise, pick authoritative version:\n878\t    ///    - Highest `_miroir_updated_at` wins\n879\t    ///    - Tiebreak: newest node task_uid\n880\t    /// 4. Write authoritative version to all replicas that disagree\n881\t    /// 5. Tag with `_miroir_origin: antientropy` for CDC suppression\n882\t    ///\n883\t    /// Returns the number of repairs performed (0-2).\n884\t    async fn repair_divergent_pk(\n885\t        &self,\n886\t        shard_id: u32,\n887\t        primary_key: &str,\n888\t        reference_node: &NodeId,\n889\t        reference_address: &str,\n890\t        target_node: &NodeId,\n891\t        target_address: &str,\n892\t    ) -> Result<u32> {\n893\t        debug!(\n894\t            \"Repairing PK {} in shard {} (reference: {}, target: {})\",\n895\t            primary_key, shard_id, reference_node, target_node\n896\t        );\n897\t\n898\t        // Step 1: Fetch document from both replicas\n899\t        let ref_doc = self\n900\t            .fetch_document_by_pk(reference_node, reference_address, shard_id, primary_key)\n901\t            .await?;\n902\t\n903\t        let target_doc = self\n904\t            .fetch_document_by_pk(target_node, target_address, shard_id, primary_key)\n905\t            .await?;\n906\t\n907\t        // Step 2: Check for TTL expiration (plan §13.14 interaction)\n908\t        // If ANY replica has an expired document, DELETE from all replicas\n909\t        let now_ms = millis_now();\n910\t        let ref_expired = ref_doc\n911\t            .as_ref()\n912\t            .and_then(|d| d.get(\"_miroir_expires_at\"))\n913\t            .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n914\t            .map_or(false, |expires| expires <= now_ms);\n915\t\n916\t        let target_expired = target_doc\n917\t            .as_ref()\n918\t            .and_then(|d| d.get(\"_miroir_expires_at\"))\n919\t            .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n920\t            .map_or(false, |expires| expires <= now_ms);\n921\t\n922\t        if ref_expired || target_expired {\n923\t            info!(\n924\t                \"PK {} has expired document (ref_expired={}, target_expired={}), deleting from all replicas\",\n925\t                primary_key, ref_expired, target_expired\n926\t            );\n927\t\n928\t            // Delete from all replicas\n929\t            let mut deletions = 0u32;\n930\t            if ref_doc.is_some() {\n931\t                self.delete_document_by_pk(reference_node, reference_address, primary_key)\n932\t                    .await?;\n933\t                deletions += 1;\n934\t            }\n935\t            if target_doc.is_some() {\n936\t                self.delete_document_by_pk(target_node, target_address, primary_key)\n937\t                    .await?;\n938\t                deletions += 1;\n939\t            }\n940\t\n941\t            return Ok(deletions);\n942\t        }\n943\t\n944\t        // Step 3: Pick authoritative version (highest _miroir_updated_at)\n945\t        let (authoritative_doc, authoritative_node) = match (&ref_doc, &target_doc) {\n946\t            (None, None) => {\n947\t                warn!(\"PK {} not found on either replica, nothing to repair\", primary_key);\n948\t                return Ok(0);\n949\t            }\n950\t            (Some(doc), None) => {\n951\t                debug!(\"PK {} only exists on reference node\", primary_key);\n952\t                (doc.clone(), reference_node.clone())\n953\t            }\n954\t            (None, Some(doc)) => {\n955\t                debug!(\"PK {} only exists on target node\", primary_key);\n956\t                (doc.clone(), target_node.clone())\n957\t            }\n958\t            (Some(ref_doc_val), Some(target_doc_val)) => {\n959\t                // Both exist - compare _miroir_updated_at\n960\t                let ref_updated = ref_doc_val\n961\t                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n962\t                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n963\t                    .unwrap_or(0);\n964\t\n965\t                let target_updated = target_doc_val\n966\t                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n967\t                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n968\t                    .unwrap_or(0);\n969\t\n970\t                if ref_updated >= target_updated {\n971\t                    debug!(\n972\t                        \"PK {} reference node wins (updated_at: {} vs {})\",\n973\t                        primary_key, ref_updated, target_updated\n974\t                    );\n975\t                    (ref_doc_val.clone(), reference_node.clone())\n976\t                } else {\n977\t                    debug!(\n978\t                        \"PK {} target node wins (updated_at: {} vs {})\",\n979\t                        primary_key, target_updated, ref_updated\n980\t                    );\n981\t                    (target_doc_val.clone(), target_node.clone())\n982\t                }\n983\t            }\n984\t        };\n985\t\n986\t        // Step 4: Write authoritative version to replicas that disagree\n987\t        let mut repairs_performed = 0u32;\n988\t\n989\t        // Check if reference needs repair\n990\t        if ref_doc.as_ref() != Some(&authoritative_doc) {\n991\t            if let Err(e) = self\n992\t                .write_document_with_origin(\n993\t                    reference_node,\n994\t                    reference_address,\n995\t                    &authoritative_doc,\n996\t                )\n997\t                .await\n998\t            {\n999\t                error!(\"Failed to write repair to reference node {}: {}\", reference_node, e);\n1000\t            } else {\n1001\t                repairs_performed += 1;\n1002\t                debug!(\"Repaired PK {} on reference node {}\", primary_key, reference_node);\n1003\t            }\n1004\t        }\n1005\t\n1006\t        // Check if target needs repair\n1007\t        if target_doc.as_ref() != Some(&authoritative_doc) {\n1008\t            if let Err(e) = self\n1009\t                .write_document_with_origin(target_node, target_address, &authoritative_doc)\n1010\t                .await\n1011\t            {\n1012\t                error!(\"Failed to write repair to target node {}: {}\", target_node, e);\n1013\t            } else {\n1014\t                repairs_performed += 1;\n1015\t                debug!(\"Repaired PK {} on target node {}\", primary_key, target_node);\n1016\t            }\n1017\t        }\n1018\t\n1019\t        if repairs_performed > 0 {\n1020\t            info!(\n1021\t                \"Repaired PK {} in shard {} on {} replica(s)\",\n1022\t                primary_key, shard_id, repairs_performed\n1023\t            );\n1024\t        }\n1025\t\n1026\t        Ok(repairs_performed)\n1027\t    }\n1028\t\n1029\t    /// Pick the authoritative document between two versions (plan §13.8 step 3).\n1030\t    ///\n1031\t    /// # Selection Logic\n1032\t    ///\n1033\t    /// 1. Highest `_miroir_updated_at` wins\n1034\t    /// 2. Tiebreak: newest node task_uid (if available)\n1035\t    /// 3. Final tiebreak: deterministic content hash comparison\n1036\t    ///\n1037\t    /// Returns `Some(&authoritative_doc)` if one or both docs exist, `None` if both are None.\n1038\t    pub fn pick_authoritative_doc<'a>(\n1039\t        &'a self,\n1040\t        doc_a: &'a Value,\n1041\t        doc_b: &'a Value,\n1042\t    ) -> Option<&'a Value> {\n1043\t        match (doc_a.is_null(), doc_b.is_null()) {\n1044\t            (true, true) => None,\n1045\t            (true, false) => Some(doc_b),\n1046\t            (false, true) => Some(doc_a),\n1047\t            (false, false) => {\n1048\t                // Both exist - compare _miroir_updated_at\n1049\t                let updated_a = doc_a\n1050\t                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n1051\t                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n1052\t                    .unwrap_or(0);\n1053\t\n1054\t                let updated_b = doc_b\n1055\t                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n1056\t                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n1057\t                    .unwrap_or(0);\n1058\t\n1059\t                if updated_a > updated_b {\n1060\t                    Some(doc_a)\n1061\t                } else if updated_b > updated_a {\n1062\t                    Some(doc_b)\n1063\t                } else {\n1064\t                    // Tie - use content hash for deterministic selection\n1065\t                    let hash_a = Self::compute_content_hash(doc_a);\n1066\t                    let hash_b = Self::compute_content_hash(doc_b);\n1067\t                    if hash_a >= hash_b {\n1068\t                        Some(doc_a)\n1069\t                    } else {\n1070\t                        Some(doc_b)\n1071\t                    }\n1072\t                }\n1073\t            }\n1074\t        }\n1075\t    }\n1076\t\n1077\t    /// Fetch a single document by primary key from a node.\n1078\t    async fn fetch_document_by_pk(\n1079\t        &self,\n1080\t        node_id: &NodeId,\n1081\t        address: &str,\n1082\t        shard_id: u32,\n1083\t        primary_key: &str,\n1084\t    ) -> Result<Option<Value>> {\n1085\t        // Build filter to find the document by PK and shard\n1086\t        let filter = serde_json::json!({\n1087\t            \"_miroir_shard\": shard_id,\n1088\t            \"id\": primary_key,\n1089\t        });\n1090\t\n1091\t        let request = FetchDocumentsRequest {\n1092\t            index_uid: self.config.index_uid.clone(),\n1093\t            filter,\n1094\t            limit: 1,\n1095\t            offset: 0,\n1096\t        };\n1097\t\n1098\t        match self\n1099\t            .node_client\n1100\t            .fetch_documents(node_id, address, &request)\n1101\t            .await\n1102\t        {\n1103\t            Ok(response) => {\n1104\t                if let Some(doc) = response.results.first() {\n1105\t                    Ok(Some(doc.clone()))\n1106\t                } else {\n1107\t                    Ok(None)\n1108\t                }\n1109\t            }\n1110\t            Err(e) => {\n1111\t                // Document not found is not an error for anti-entropy\n1112\t                debug!(\"PK {} not found on node {}: {:?}\", primary_key, node_id, e);\n1113\t                Ok(None)\n1114\t            }\n1115\t        }\n1116\t    }\n1117\t\n1118\t    /// Write a document with the anti-entropy origin tag for CDC suppression.\n1119\t    async fn write_document_with_origin(\n1120\t        &self,\n1121\t        node_id: &NodeId,\n1122\t        address: &str,\n1123\t        document: &Value,\n1124\t    ) -> Result<()> {\n1125\t        let request = WriteRequest {\n1126\t            index_uid: self.config.index_uid.clone(),\n1127\t            documents: vec![document.clone()],\n1128\t            primary_key: None,\n1129\t            origin: Some(ORIGIN_ANTIENTROPY.to_string()),\n1130\t        };\n1131\t\n1132\t        self.node_client\n1133\t            .write_documents(node_id, address, &request)\n1134\t            .await\n1135\t            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"write failed: {:?}\", e)))?;\n1136\t\n1137\t        Ok(())\n1138\t    }\n1139\t\n1140\t    /// Delete a document by primary key Anti-entropy reconciler module (plan §13.8).\n//!\n//! Detects and repairs replica drift using the fingerprint → diff → repair pipeline.\n//! Resolves Open Problem #1 (dual-write safety) by continuously reconciling\n//! replicas and catching any missed writes.\n//!\n//! # CDC Origin Tag (plan §13.13)\n//!\n//! Repair writes must be tagged with `origin=\"antientropy\"` so they are suppressed\n//! from CDC by default (unless `emit_internal_writes` is true).\n//!\n//! When constructing `WriteRequest` for repair writes, set:\n//! ```ignore\n//! use miroir_core::cdc::ORIGIN_ANTIENTROPY;\n//! self.config.ttl_enabled = enabled;\n    }\n\n    /// Compute bucket ID for a primary key (plan §13.8 step 2).\n    ///\n    /// Uses pk-hash modulo BUCKET_COUNT to isolate divergence to ~0.4% of PK space.\n    /// This is reused by §13.1 reshard verify with PK-keyed bucketing.\n    pub fn bucket_for_primary_key(primary_key: &str) -> usize {\n        let mut hasher = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n        hasher.write(primary_key.as_bytes());\n        (hasher.finish() as usize) % BUCKET_COUNT\n    }\n\n    /// Compute the canonical content hash of a document.\n    ///\n    /// The canonical form excludes internal Miroir fields (_miroir_*, _rankingScore)\n    /// and serializes with sorted keys for deterministic hashing.\n    pub fn compute_content_hash(document: &Value) -> u64 {\n        // Remove internal fields to get canonical content\n        let mut canonical = document.clone();\n        if let Some(obj) = canonical.as_object_mut() {\n            // Remove all _miroir_* fields\n            obj.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n            // Remove _rankingScore (not content, used for scoring)\n            obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n        }\n\n        // Serialize with sorted keys for deterministic output\n        let canonical_json = if let Some(obj) = canonical.as_object() {\n            // Use BTreeMap to sort keys\n            let sorted: BTreeMap<_, _> = obj.iter().collect();\n            serde_json::to_string(&sorted).unwrap_or_else(|_| \"{}\".to_string())\n        } else {\n            serde_json::to_string(&canonical).unwrap_or_else(|_| \"{}\".to_string())\n        };\n\n        // Hash using xxh3 (xxhash family, same as router)\n        let mut hasher = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n        hasher.write(canonical_json.as_bytes());\n        hasher.finish()\n    }\n\n    /// Check if a document is expired (plan §13.14 interaction).\n    ///\n    /// Returns true if the document has an expires_at field that is in the past.\n    /// Expired documents are treated as logically deleted by anti-entropy\n    /// to prevent zombie resurrection.\n    fn is_document_expired(document: &Value) -> bool {\n        if let Some(expires_at) = document.get(\"_miroir_expires_at\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()) {\n            let now_ms = SystemTime::now()\n                .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)\n                .unwrap_or_default()\n                .as_millis() as u64;\n            expires_at <= now_ms\n        } else {\n            false\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Fingerprint a single shard on a node (plan §13.8 step 1).\n    ///\n    /// Iterates all documents with filter=_miroir_shard={id}, computes\n    /// hash(primary_key || content_hash) for each, and folds into a\n    /// streaming xxh3 digest. Also computes per-bucket hashes for diff.\n    pub async fn fingerprint_shard(\n        &self,\n        node_id: &NodeId,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        index_uid: &str,\n        address: &str,\n    ) -> Result<ShardFingerprint> {\n        let batch_size = self.config.fingerprint_batch_size as usize;\n        let mut offset = 0u32;\n        let mut document_count = 0u64;\n        let mut hasher = XxHash64::with_seed(shard_id as u64); // Shard-seeded digest\n\n        // Per-bucket hashers for granular diff (plan §13.8 step 2)\n        let mut bucket_hashers: Vec<XxHash64> = (0..BUCKET_COUNT)\n            .map(|_| XxHash64::with_seed(shard_id as u64))\n            .collect();\n\n        // Paginated iteration through documents\n        loop {\n            let filter = serde_json::json!({ \"_miroir_shard\": shard_id });\n            let request = FetchDocumentsRequest {\n                index_uid: index_uid.to_string(),\n                filter,\n                limit: batch_size as u32,\n                offset,\n            };\n\n            let response: FetchDocumentsResponse = self\n                .node_client\n                .fetch_documents(node_id, address, &request)\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"fetch failed: {:?}\", e)))?;\n\n            if response.results.is_empty() {\n                break; // No more documents\n            }\n\n            for doc in &response.results {\n                // Skip expired documents (plan §13.14 interaction)\n                // Treats them as logically deleted to prevent zombie resurrection\n                if self.config.ttl_enabled && Self::is_document_expired(doc) {\n                    debug!(\n                        shard_id,\n                        primary_key = doc.get(\"id\").or(doc.get(\"_id\")).and_then(|v| v.as_str()).unwrap_or(\"\"),\n                        \"Skipping expired document in anti-entropy fingerprint\"\n                    );\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                // Extract primary key\n                let primary_key = doc\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .or(doc.get(\"_id\"))\n                    .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\");\n\n                // Compute content hash\n                let content_hash = Self::compute_content_hash(doc);\n\n                // Fold: hash(primary_key || content_hash) into digest\n                let mut pk_hasher = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n                pk_hasher.write(primary_key.as_bytes());\n                pk_hasher.write_u64(content_hash);\n                let doc_hash = pk_hasher.finish();\n\n                // Fold into shard digest\n                hasher.write_u64(doc_hash);\n                document_count += 1;\n\n                // Fold into bucket digest for granular diff\n                let bucket_id = Self::bucket_for_primary_key(primary_key);\n                bucket_hashers[bucket_id].write_u64(doc_hash);\n            }\n\n            offset += batch_size as u32;\n\n            // Self-throttle: small sleep between batches to target <2% CPU\n            // (In production, this would be adaptive based on CPU metrics)\n            tokio::time::sleep(tokio::time::Duration::from_millis(10)).await;\n        }\n\n        let merkle_root = format!(\"xxh3:{}\", hasher.finish());\n\n        // Extract per-bucket hashes\n        let bucket_hashes: Vec<String> = bucket_hashers\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|h| format!(\"xxh3:{}\", h.finish()))\n            .collect();\n\n        debug!(\n            \"Fingerprinted shard {} on node {}: {} documents, root {}\",\n            shard_id, node_id, document_count, merkle_root\n        );\n\n        Ok(ShardFingerprint {\n            shard_id,\n            node_id: node_id.to_string(),\n            merkle_root,\n            document_count,\n            bucket_hashes,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Find divergent buckets between two fingerprints (plan §13.8 step 2).\n    ///\n    /// Returns bucket IDs where the per-bucket hashes differ.\n    /// Each bucket isolates divergence to ~0.4% of the PK space.\n    pub fn diff_fingerprints(\n        &self,\n        fp_a: &ShardFingerprint,\n        fp_b: &ShardFingerprint,\n    ) -> Vec<usize> {\n        let mut divergent = Vec::new();\n\n        if fp_a.bucket_hashes.len() != BUCKET_COUNT || fp_b.bucket_hashes.len() != BUCKET_COUNT {\n            // Fallback: if bucket hashes aren't computed, treat all buckets as divergent\n            warn!(\n                \"Bucket hashes not computed, treating all {} buckets as divergent\",\n                BUCKET_COUNT\n            );\n            return (0..BUCKET_COUNT).collect();\n        }\n\n        for (bucket_id, (hash_a, hash_b)) in fp_a\n            .bucket_hashes\n            .iter()\n            .zip(fp_b.bucket_hashes.iter())\n            .enumerate()\n        {\n            if hash_a != hash_b {\n                divergent.push(bucket_id);\n            }\n        }\n\n        divergent\n    }\n\n    /// Fetch all primary keys in a specific bucket (plan §13.8 step 2).\n    ///\n    /// Returns a map of primary key to content hash for all documents\n    /// in the given bucket on the specified replica.\n    pub async fn fetch_bucket_pks(\n        &self,\n        node_id: &NodeId,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        bucket_id: usize,\n        index_uid: &str,\n        address: &str,\n    ) -> Result<HashMap<String, u64>> {\n        let batch_size = self.config.fingerprint_batch_size as usize;\n        let mut offset = 0u32;\n        let mut bucket_pks = HashMap::new();\n\n        loop {\n            let filter = serde_json::json!({ \"_miroir_shard\": shard_id });\n            let request = FetchDocumentsRequest {\n                index_uid: index_uid.to_string(),\n                filter,\n                limit: batch_size as u32,\n                offset,\n            };\n\n            let response: FetchDocumentsResponse = self\n                .node_client\n                .fetch_documents(node_id, address, &request)\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"fetch failed: {:?}\", e)))?;\n\n            if response.results.is_empty() {\n                break;\n            }\n\n            for doc in &response.results {\n                // Skip expired documents (plan §13.14 interaction)\n                if self.config.ttl_enabled && Self::is_document_expired(doc) {\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                let primary_key = doc\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .or(doc.get(\"_id\"))\n                    .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\");\n\n                // Check if this document belongs to the target bucket\n                let doc_bucket = Self::bucket_for_primary_key(primary_key);\n                if doc_bucket == bucket_id {\n                    let content_hash = Self::compute_content_hash(doc);\n                    bucket_pks.insert(primary_key.to_string(), content_hash);\n                }\n            }\n\n            offset += batch_size as u32;\n            tokio::time::sleep(tokio::time::Duration::from_millis(10)).await;\n        }\n\n        Ok(bucket_pks)\n    }\n\n    /// Compare replicas within a divergent bucket to find specific PK differences.\n    ///\n    /// Returns a ReplicaDiff listing:\n    /// - PKs only in replica A\n    /// - PKs only in replica B\n    /// - PKs with different content hashes\n    pub async fn compare_bucket_replicas(\n        &self,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        bucket_id: usize,\n        node_a: &NodeId,\n        address_a: &str,\n        node_b: &NodeId,\n        address_b: &str,\n        index_uid: &str,\n    ) -> Result<ReplicaDiff> {\n        let pks_a = self\n            .fetch_bucket_pks(node_a, shard_id, bucket_id, index_uid, address_a)\n            .await?;\n        let pks_b = self\n            .fetch_bucket_pks(node_b, shard_id, bucket_id, index_uid, address_b)\n            .await?;\n\n        let mut a_only = Vec::new();\n        let mut b_only = Vec::new();\n        let mut mismatched = Vec::new();\n\n        // Find PKs only in A or with mismatched content\n        for (pk, hash_a) in &pks_a {\n            match pks_b.get(pk) {\n                Some(hash_b) if hash_b != hash_a => {\n                    mismatched.push(pk.clone());\n                }\n                None => {\n                    a_only.push(pk.clone());\n                }\n                _ => {}\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Find PKs only in B\n        for pk in pks_b.keys() {\n            if !pks_a.contains_key(pk) {\n                b_only.push(pk.clone());\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(ReplicaDiff {\n            shard_id,\n            a_only_pks: a_only,\n            b_only_pks: b_only,\n            mismatched_pks: mismatched,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Run a single reconciliation pass.\n    pub async fn run_pass(&self) -> Result<ReconcilerPass> {\n        let mut pass = ReconcilerPass {\n            started_at: millis_now(),\n            completed_at: 0,\n            shards_scanned: 0,\n            shards_with_drift: 0,\n            repairs_performed: 0,\n            errors: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        // Set as current pass\n        {\n            let mut current = self.current_pass.write().await;\n            *current = Some(pass.clone());\n        }\n\n        let topology = self.topology.read().await;\n        let shard_count = topology.shards;\n        let replica_groups = topology.groups().count() as u32;\n\n        // Determine which shards to scan\n        let all_shards: Vec<u32> = (0..shard_count).collect();\n        let shards_to_scan = if let (Some(replica_group_id), Some(num_pods)) =\n            (self.replica_group_id, self.num_pods)\n        {\n            // Mode A scaling: filter to rendezvous-owned shards\n            all_shards\n                .into_iter()\n                .filter(|shard_id| {\n                    // Shard belongs to this pod if shard_id % num_pods == replica_group_id\n                    (*shard_id % num_pods) == replica_group_id\n                })\n                .collect()\n        } else if self.config.shards_per_pass == 0 {\n            // Scan all shards\n            all_shards\n        } else {\n            // Scan a subset (for throttling)\n            all_shards\n                .into_iter()\n                .take(self.config.shards_per_pass as usize)\n                .collect()\n        };\n\n        info!(\n            \"Anti-entropy pass starting: {} shards to scan\",\n            shards_to_scan.len()\n        );\n\n        // Track total mismatches found\n        let mut total_mismatches = 0u32;\n\n        // Scan each shard\n        for shard_id in shards_to_scan {\n            match self.scan_shard(&topology, shard_id).await {\n                Ok((drift_detected, repairs, mismatches)) => {\n                    pass.shards_scanned += 1;\n                    if drift_detected {\n                        pass.shards_with_drift += 1;\n                    }\n                    pass.repairs_performed += repairs;\n                    total_mismatches += mismatches;\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    pass.errors.push(format!(\"shard {}: {}\", shard_id, e));\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Self-throttle: sleep between shards to target <2% CPU\n            tokio::time::sleep(tokio::time::Duration::from_millis(100)).await;\n        }\n\n        pass.completed_at = millis_now();\n\n        // Emit metrics if callback is configured\n        if let Some(ref callback) = self.metrics_callback {\n            callback(\n                \"miroir_antientropy_shards_scanned_total\",\n                pass.shards_scanned as u64,\n            );\n            callback(\n                \"miroir_antientropy_mismatches_found_total\",\n                total_mismatches as u64,\n            );\n            callback(\n                \"miroir_antientropy_docs_repaired_total\",\n                pass.repairs_performed as u64,\n            );\n            callback(\n                \"miroir_antientropy_last_scan_completed_seconds\",\n                pass.completed_at / 1000,\n            );\n        }\n\n        // Archive pass\n        {\n            let mut history = self.pass_history.write().await;\n            history.push(pass.clone());\n            // Keep last 100 passes\n            if history.len() > 100 {\n                history.remove(0);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Clear current pass\n        {\n            let mut current = self.current_pass.write().await;\n            *current = None;\n        }\n\n        info!(\n            \"Anti-entropy pass completed: {} shards scanned, {} with drift, {} repairs\",\n            pass.shards_scanned, pass.shards_with_drift, pass.repairs_performed\n        );\n\n        Ok(pass)\n    }\n\n    /// Scan a single shard for drift.\n    ///\n    /// Returns (drift_detected, repairs_performed, mismatches_found).\n    async fn scan_shard(&self, topology: &Topology, shard_id: u32) -> Result<(bool, u32, u32)> {\n        // For each replica group, get the assigned nodes\n        let mut fingerprints = Vec::new();\n\n        for group in topology.groups() {\n            let assigned = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n            for node_id in assigned {\n                // Look up node address from topology\n                let topology_guard = self.topology.read().await;\n                let node = topology_guard\n                    .node(&node_id)\n                    .ok_or_else(|| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"node {} not found\", node_id)))?;\n\n                if !node.is_healthy() {\n                    warn!(\"Node {} is not healthy, skipping fingerprint\", node_id);\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                let address = node.address.clone();\n                drop(topology_guard);\n\n                match self\n                    .fingerprint_shard(&node_id, shard_id, &self.config.index_uid, &address)\n                    .await\n                {\n                    Ok(fp) => fingerprints.push((node_id.clone(), address, fp)),\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        warn!(\n                            \"Failed to fingerprint shard {} on node {}: {}\",\n                            shard_id, node_id, e\n                        );\n                        // Continue with other nodes\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if fingerprints.is_empty() {\n            // No readable replicas\n            return Ok((false, 0, 0));\n        }\n\n        // Compare fingerprints\n        let (ref_node_id, ref_address, reference) = &fingerprints[0];\n        let mut drift_detected = false;\n        let mut repairs_performed = 0u32;\n        let mut mismatches_found = 0u32;\n\n        for (node_id, address, fp) in &fingerprints[1..] {\n            if fp.merkle_root != reference.merkle_root {\n                drift_detected = true;\n                debug!(\n                    \"Shard {} drift detected: node {} has different merkle root\",\n                    shard_id, node_id\n                );\n\n                if self.config.auto_repair {\n                    // Perform detailed diff and repair\n                    match self\n                        .repair_shard(\n                            shard_id,\n                            ref_node_id,\n                            ref_address,\n                            reference,\n                            node_id,\n                            address,\n                            fp,\n                        )\n                        .await\n                    {\n                        Ok((repairs, mismatches)) => {\n                            repairs_performed += repairs;\n                            mismatches_found += mismatches;\n                        }\n                        Err(e) => {\n                            error!(\n                                \"Failed to repair shard {} on node {}: {}\",\n                                shard_id, node_id, e\n                            );\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok((drift_detected, repairs_performed, mismatches_found))\n    }\n\n    /// Repair a shard by comparing replicas and applying fixes (plan §13.8 step 3).\n    ///\n    /// Returns (repairs_performed, mismatches_found).\n    async fn repair_shard(\n        &self,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        reference_node: &NodeId,\n        reference_address: &str,\n        reference_fp: &ShardFingerprint,\n        target_node: &NodeId,\n        target_address: &str,\n        target_fp: &ShardFingerprint,\n    ) -> Result<(u32, u32)> {\n        debug!(\n            \"Repairing shard {} on node {} (reference: node {})\",\n            shard_id, target_node, reference_node\n        );\n\n        // Step 1: Find divergent buckets using per-bucket hashes (plan §13.8 step 2)\n        let divergent_buckets = self.diff_fingerprints(reference_fp, target_fp);\n\n        if divergent_buckets.is_empty() {\n            // No bucket-level divergence (shouldn't happen if merkle roots differ)\n            warn!(\n                \"Shard {} merkle roots differ but no bucket divergence found\",\n                shard_id\n            );\n            return Ok((0, 0));\n        }\n\n        debug!(\n            \"Shard {} has {} divergent buckets out of {}\",\n            shard_id,\n            divergent_buckets.len(),\n            BUCKET_COUNT\n        );\n\n        let mut total_repairs = 0u32;\n        let mut total_mismatches = 0u32;\n\n        // Step 2: For each divergent bucket, enumerate divergent PKs\n        for bucket_id in divergent_buckets {\n            match self\n                .compare_bucket_replicas(\n                    shard_id,\n                    bucket_id,\n                    reference_node,\n                    reference_address,\n                    target_node,\n                    target_address,\n                    &self.config.index_uid,\n                )\n                .await\n            {\n                Ok(diff) => {\n                    let total_divergent =\n                        diff.a_only_pks.len() + diff.b_only_pks.len() + diff.mismatched_pks.len();\n                    total_mismatches += total_divergent as u32;\n\n                    if total_divergent > 0 {\n                        debug!(\n                            \"Bucket {} in shard {}: {} divergent PKs ({} A-only, {} B-only, {} mismatched)\",\n                            bucket_id,\n                            shard_id,\n                            total_divergent,\n                            diff.a_only_pks.len(),\n                            diff.b_only_pks.len(),\n                            diff.mismatched_pks.len()\n                        );\n\n                        // Step 3: For each divergent PK, apply repair (plan §13.8 step 3)\n                        // Collect all divergent PKs\n                        let mut all_divergent_pks = Vec::new();\n                        all_divergent_pks.extend(diff.a_only_pks.iter().cloned());\n                        all_divergent_pks.extend(diff.b_only_pks.iter().cloned());\n                        all_divergent_pks.extend(diff.mismatched_pks.iter().cloned());\n\n                        // Repair each divergent PK\n                        for pk in all_divergent_pks {\n                            match self\n                                .repair_divergent_pk(\n                                    shard_id,\n                                    &pk,\n                                    reference_node,\n                                    reference_address,\n                                    target_node,\n                                    target_address,\n                                )\n                                .await\n                            {\n                                Ok(repairs) => {\n                                    total_repairs += repairs;\n                                }\n                                Err(e) => {\n                                    error!(\n                                        \"Failed to repair PK {} in shard {}: {}\",\n                                        pk, shard_id, e\n                                    );\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    warn!(\n                        \"Failed to compare bucket {} in shard {}: {}\",\n                        bucket_id, shard_id, e\n                    );\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok((total_repairs, total_mismatches))\n    }\n\n    /// Repair a single divergent primary key (plan §13.8 step 3).\n    ///\n    /// # Repair Logic (plan §13.8 step 3)\n    ///\n    /// For each divergent PK:\n    /// 1. Read document from each replica\n    /// 2. Check for TTL expiration:\n    ///    - If ANY replica has `_miroir_expires_at <= now`: DELETE from all replicas\n    ///    - This prevents zombie resurrection (plan §13.14 interaction)\n    /// 3. Otherwise, pick authoritative version:\n    ///    - Highest `_miroir_updated_at` wins\n    ///    - Tiebreak: newest node task_uid\n    /// 4. Write authoritative version to all replicas that disagree\n    /// 5. Tag with `_miroir_origin: antientropy` for CDC suppression\n    ///\n    /// Returns the number of repairs performed (0-2).\n    async fn repair_divergent_pk(\n        &self,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        primary_key: &str,\n        reference_node: &NodeId,\n        reference_address: &str,\n        target_node: &NodeId,\n        target_address: &str,\n    ) -> Result<u32> {\n        debug!(\n            \"Repairing PK {} in shard {} (reference: {}, target: {})\",\n            primary_key, shard_id, reference_node, target_node\n        );\n\n        // Step 1: Fetch document from both replicas\n        let ref_doc = self\n            .fetch_document_by_pk(reference_node, reference_address, shard_id, primary_key)\n            .await?;\n\n        let target_doc = self\n            .fetch_document_by_pk(target_node, target_address, shard_id, primary_key)\n            .await?;\n\n        // Step 2: Check for TTL expiration (plan §13.14 interaction)\n        // If ANY replica has an expired document, DELETE from all replicas\n        let now_ms = millis_now();\n        let ref_expired = ref_doc\n            .as_ref()\n            .and_then(|d| d.get(\"_miroir_expires_at\"))\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n            .map_or(false, |expires| expires <= now_ms);\n\n        let target_expired = target_doc\n            .as_ref()\n            .and_then(|d| d.get(\"_miroir_expires_at\"))\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n            .map_or(false, |expires| expires <= now_ms);\n\n        if ref_expired || target_expired {\n            info!(\n                \"PK {} has expired document (ref_expired={}, target_expired={}), deleting from all replicas\",\n                primary_key, ref_expired, target_expired\n            );\n\n            // Delete from all replicas\n            let mut deletions = 0u32;\n            if ref_doc.is_some() {\n                self.delete_document_by_pk(reference_node, reference_address, primary_key)\n                    .await?;\n                deletions += 1;\n            }\n            if target_doc.is_some() {\n                self.delete_document_by_pk(target_node, target_address, primary_key)\n                    .await?;\n                deletions += 1;\n            }\n\n            return Ok(deletions);\n        }\n\n        // Step 3: Pick authoritative version (highest _miroir_updated_at)\n        let (authoritative_doc, authoritative_node) = match (&ref_doc, &target_doc) {\n            (None, None) => {\n                warn!(\"PK {} not found on either replica, nothing to repair\", primary_key);\n                return Ok(0);\n            }\n            (Some(doc), None) => {\n                debug!(\"PK {} only exists on reference node\", primary_key);\n                (doc.clone(), reference_node.clone())\n            }\n            (None, Some(doc)) => {\n                debug!(\"PK {} only exists on target node\", primary_key);\n                (doc.clone(), target_node.clone())\n            }\n            (Some(ref_doc_val), Some(target_doc_val)) => {\n                // Both exist - compare _miroir_updated_at\n                let ref_updated = ref_doc_val\n                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0);\n\n                let target_updated = target_doc_val\n                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0);\n\n                if ref_updated >= target_updated {\n                    debug!(\n                        \"PK {} reference node wins (updated_at: {} vs {})\",\n                        primary_key, ref_updated, target_updated\n                    );\n                    (ref_doc_val.clone(), reference_node.clone())\n                } else {\n                    debug!(\n                        \"PK {} target node wins (updated_at: {} vs {})\",\n                        primary_key, target_updated, ref_updated\n                    );\n                    (target_doc_val.clone(), target_node.clone())\n                }\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Step 4: Write authoritative version to replicas that disagree\n        let mut repairs_performed = 0u32;\n\n        // Check if reference needs repair\n        if ref_doc.as_ref() != Some(&authoritative_doc) {\n            if let Err(e) = self\n                .write_document_with_origin(\n                    reference_node,\n                    reference_address,\n                    &authoritative_doc,\n                )\n                .await\n            {\n                error!(\"Failed to write repair to reference node {}: {}\", reference_node, e);\n            } else {\n                repairs_performed += 1;\n                debug!(\"Repaired PK {} on reference node {}\", primary_key, reference_node);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check if target needs repair\n        if target_doc.as_ref() != Some(&authoritative_doc) {\n            if let Err(e) = self\n                .write_document_with_origin(target_node, target_address, &authoritative_doc)\n                .await\n            {\n                error!(\"Failed to write repair to target node {}: {}\", target_node, e);\n            } else {\n                repairs_performed += 1;\n                debug!(\"Repaired PK {} on target node {}\", primary_key, target_node);\n            }\n        }\n\n        if repairs_performed > 0 {\n            info!(\n                \"Repaired PK {} in shard {} on {} replica(s)\",\n                primary_key, shard_id, repairs_performed\n            );\n        }\n\n        Ok(repairs_performed)\n    }\n\n    /// Pick the authoritative document between two versions (plan §13.8 step 3).\n    ///\n    /// # Selection Logic\n    ///\n    /// 1. Highest `_miroir_updated_at` wins\n    /// 2. Tiebreak: newest node task_uid (if available)\n    /// 3. Final tiebreak: deterministic content hash comparison\n    ///\n    /// Returns `Some(&authoritative_doc)` if one or both docs exist, `None` if both are None.\n    pub fn pick_authoritative_doc<'a>(\n        &'a self,\n        doc_a: &'a Value,\n        doc_b: &'a Value,\n    ) -> Option<&'a Value> {\n        match (doc_a.is_null(), doc_b.is_null()) {\n            (true, true) => None,\n            (true, false) => Some(doc_b),\n            (false, true) => Some(doc_a),\n            (false, false) => {\n                // Both exist - compare _miroir_updated_at\n                let updated_a = doc_a\n                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0);\n\n                let updated_b = doc_b\n                    .get(&self.config.updated_at_field)\n                    .and_then(|v| v.as_u64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0);\n\n                if updated_a > updated_b {\n                    Some(doc_a)\n                } else if updated_b > updated_a {\n                    Some(doc_b)\n                } else {\n                    // Tie - use content hash for deterministic selection\n                    let hash_a = Self::compute_content_hash(doc_a);\n                    let hash_b = Self::compute_content_hash(doc_b);\n                    if hash_a >= hash_b {\n                        Some(doc_a)\n                    } else {\n                        Some(doc_b)\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Fetch a single document by primary key from a node.\n    async fn fetch_document_by_pk(\n        &self,\n        node_id: &NodeId,\n        address: &str,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        primary_key: &str,\n    ) -> Result<Option<Value>> {\n        // Build filter to find the document by PK and shard\n        let filter = serde_json::json!({\n            \"_miroir_shard\": shard_id,\n            \"id\": primary_key,\n        });\n\n        let request = FetchDocumentsRequest {\n            index_uid: self.config.index_uid.clone(),\n            filter,\n            limit: 1,\n            offset: 0,\n        };\n\n        match self\n            .node_client\n            .fetch_documents(node_id, address, &request)\n            .await\n        {\n            Ok(response) => {\n                if let Some(doc) = response.results.first() {\n                    Ok(Some(doc.clone()))\n                } else {\n                    Ok(None)\n                }\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                // Document not found is not an error for anti-entropy\n                debug!(\"PK {} not found on node {}: {:?}\", primary_key, node_id, e);\n                Ok(None)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Write a document with the anti-entropy origin tag for CDC suppression.\n    async fn write_document_with_origin(\n        &self,\n        node_id: &NodeId,\n        address: &str,\n        document: &Value,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let request = WriteRequest {\n            index_uid: self.config.index_uid.clone(),\n            documents: vec![document.clone()],\n            primary_key: None,\n            origin: Some(ORIGIN_ANTIENTROPY.to_string()),\n        };\n\n        self.node_client\n            .write_documents(node_id, address, &request)\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"write failed: {:?}\", e)))?;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Delete a document by primary key with the anti-entropy origin tag.\n    async fn delete_document_by_pk(\n        &self,\n        node_id: &NodeId,\n        address: &str,\n        primary_key: &str,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let request = for reshard verification (plan §13.1 step 4).\n    ///\n    /// Compares two indexes with potentially different shard counts (e.g., live vs shadow\n    /// during resharding). Uses PK-keyed bucketing (pk-hash % 256) which is independent\n    /// of the shard count, enabling cross-S comparison.\n    ///\n    /// Returns a ReplicaDiff listing divergent PKs across all buckets.\n    /// This reuses §13.8's bucketed-Merkle machinery but operates across indexes\n    /// rather than within a single shard.\n    pub async fn compare_index_buckets(\n        &self,\n        node_a: &NodeId,\n        address_a: &str,\n        index_a: &str,\n        shard_count_a: u32,\n        node_b: &NodeId,\n        address_b: &str,\n        index_b: &str,\n        shard_count_b: u32,\n    ) -> Result<ReplicaDiff> {\n        let mut all_a_only = Vec::new();\n        let mut all_b_only = Vec::new();\n        let mut all_mismatched = Vec::new();\n\n        // Fetch all PKs and their content hashes from both indexes, bucketed by PK\n        let bucket_pks_a = self.fetch_all_index_pks_bucketed(node_a, address_a, index_a, shard_count_a).await?;\n        let bucket_pks_b = self.fetch_all_index_pks_bucketed(node_b, address_b, index_b, shard_count_b).await?;\n\n        // Compare each bucket\n        for bucket_id in 0..BUCKET_COUNT {\n            let pks_a = &bucket_pks_a[bucket_id];\n            let pks_b = &bucket_pks_b[bucket_id];\n\n            // Find PKs only in A or with mismatched content\n            for (pk, hash_a) in pks_a {\n                match pks_b.get(pk) {\n                    Some(hash_b) if hash_b != hash_a => {\n                        all_mismatched.push(pk.clone());\n                    }\n                    None => {\n                        all_a_only.push(pk.clone());\n                    }\n                    _ => {}\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Find PKs only in B\n            for pk in pks_b.keys() {\n                if !pks_a.contains_key(pk) {\n                    all_b_only.push(pk.clone());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(ReplicaDiff {\n            shard_id: 0, // Not applicable for cross-index comparison\n            a_only_pks: all_a_only,\n            b_only_pks: all_b_only,\n            mismatched_pks: all_mismatched,\n        })\n    }\n\n .await\n                    .map_err(|e| MiroirError::Topology(format!(\"fetch failed: {:?}\", e)))?;\n\n                if response.results.is_empty() {\n                    break;\n tokio::time::sleep(tokio::time::Duration::from_millis(10)).await;\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(bucket_pks)\n    }\n\n    /// Get pass history.\n    pub async fn pass_history(&self) ->
